The following table was created as response to the SQL query
SELECT sbs_sbsname "SBS name", sbs_sbsnumber "SBS number", dtlv_name "dispersal type", dvlv_name "dispersal vector", dvglv_genname "gen. dispersal vector", dglv_genname "gen. dispersal type", byc_avgsingle "BYC avg. float. cap. (sv) [%]" FROM (SELECT ROUND(AVG(byc_singlevalue),2) AS byc_avgsingle, sbs_sbsnumber, sbs_sbsname, dtlv_name, dvlv_name, dvglv_genname, dglv_genname FROM (SELECT case when byc_median is not null then byc_median when byc_mean is not null then byc_mean when byc_minimum is not null and byc_maximum is not null then (byc_minimum + byc_maximum) / 2 when byc_minimum is not null then byc_minimum when byc_maximum is not null then byc_maximum else null end AS byc_singlevalue, sbs_sbsnumber, sbs_sbsname, dtlv_name, dvlv_name, dvglv_genname, dglv_genname FROM (SELECT sbs_dis.sbs_sbsnumber, sbs_dis.sbs_sbsname, sbs_dis.dtlv_name, sbs_dis.dvlv_name, sbs_dis.dvglv_genname, sbs_dis.dglv_genname, byc.byc_median, byc.byc_mean, byc.byc_minimum, byc.byc_maximum FROM (SELECT sbs.sbs_sbsnumber, sbs.sbs_sbsname, dis_dtlv.dtlv_name, dis_dtlv.dvlv_name, dis_dtlv.dvglv_genname, dis_dtlv.dglv_genname FROM (SELECT speciesno AS sbs_sbsnumber, fullname AS sbs_sbsname FROM (SELECT fullname, speciesno, familyname, isinledalist from (select fullname, speciesno, family as familyid, isinledalist from taxon where specieslist = 60028) natural join taxonomicfamily)) sbs LEFT JOIN (SELECT dis_dvlv.dis_sbsnumber, dtlv.dtlv_name, dis_dvlv.dvlv_name, dis_dvlv.dvglv_genname, dis_dvlv.dglv_genname FROM (SELECT dis_dvglv.dis_sbsnumber, dis_dvglv.dis_dtid, dvlv.dvlv_name, dis_dvglv.dvglv_genname, dis_dvglv.dglv_genname FROM (SELECT dis_dtglv.dis_sbsnumber, dis_dtglv.dis_dtid, dis_dtglv.dis_dvid, dvglv.dvglv_genname, dis_dtglv.dglv_genname FROM (SELECT dis.dis_sbsnumber, dis.dis_dtid, dis.dis_dvid, dis.dis_gendvid, dtglv.dglv_genname FROM (SELECT sbsnumber AS dis_sbsnumber, dispersaltypeid AS dis_dtid, dispersalvectorid AS dis_dvid, gendispvectorid AS dis_gendvid, gendisptypeid AS dis_gendtid FROM (SELECT sbsnumber, taxonid, georefid, habitattypeid, referenceid, origreferenceid, batchid, methodid, p_comment, dispersalunitid, dispersaltypeid, dispersalvectorid, dispersalunitid - mod(dispersalunitid,10) as gendispunitid, dispersaltypeid - mod(dispersaltypeid,10) as gendisptypeid, dispersalvectorid - mod(dispersalvectorid,100) as gendispvectorid, created_when, updated_when, valid, validsince, validuntil, ledaid, dispersalid FROM dispersal NATURAL JOIN taxontosbsassignment)) dis FULL JOIN (SELECT dispersaltypeid AS dglv_genid, dispersaltypename AS dglv_genname FROM (select dispersaltypeid, dispersaltypename, generaliseddispersaltype, explanation, case when lddid = 0 then 'no' when lddid = 1 then 'yes' else 'unknown' end as dispersaltypelddpotential from dispersaltype_lv)) dtglv ON dis.dis_gendtid = dtglv.dglv_genid) dis_dtglv FULL JOIN (SELECT dispersalvectorid AS dvglv_genid, dispersalvectorname AS dvglv_genname FROM (select dispersalvectorid, dispersalvectorname, longdistancedispersal from dispersalvector_lv)) dvglv ON dis_dtglv.dis_gendvid = dvglv.dvglv_genid) dis_dvglv FULL JOIN (SELECT dispersalvectorid AS dvlv_id, dispersalvectorname AS dvlv_name FROM (select dispersalvectorid, dispersalvectorname, case when longdistancedispersal = 1 then 'yes' when longdistancedispersal = 0 then 'no' else 'unknown' end as longdistancedispersal from dispersalvector_lv)) dvlv ON dis_dvglv.dis_dvid = dvlv.dvlv_id) dis_dvlv FULL JOIN (SELECT dispersaltypeid AS dtlv_id, dispersaltypename AS dtlv_name FROM (select dispersaltypeid, dispersaltypename, generaliseddispersaltype, explanation, case when lddid = 0 then 'no' when lddid = 1 then 'yes' else 'unknown' end as dispersaltypelddpotential from dispersaltype_lv)) dtlv ON dis_dvlv.dis_dtid = dtlv.dtlv_id) dis_dtlv ON sbs.sbs_sbsnumber = dis_dtlv.dis_sbsnumber) sbs_dis LEFT JOIN (SELECT sbsnumber AS byc_sbsnumber, median AS byc_median, mean AS byc_mean, minimum AS byc_minimum, maximum AS byc_maximum, valid AS byc_valid FROM (select SBSNUMBER, DISPERSALMEASUREMENTID, TIMESTEPMINUTES, TIMESTEPINTERVAL || ' - ' || TIMESTEPNAME AS TIMESTEPCODEANDNAME, N, REPLICATES, MEAN, MEDIAN, MINIMUM, MAXIMUM, STDDEVIATION, STDERROR, P_COMMENT, CREATED_WHEN, UPDATED_WHEN, BATCHID, UPDATEDWHO, REFERENCEID, METHODID, TAXONID, ORIGREFERENCEID, HABITATTYPEID, GEOREFID, VALID, VALIDSINCE, VALIDUNTIL, LEDAID, DISPERSALID, DISPERSALPOTENTIAL, ORIGINALDISPERSALVECTORVALUE, DISPERSALVECTORID, dispersalvectorid - mod(dispersalvectorid,100) as gendispvectorid, DISPERSALTYPEID, dispersaltypeid - mod(dispersaltypeid,10) as gendisptypeid,
DISPERSALUNITID, dispersalunitid - mod(dispersalunitid,10) as gendispersalunitid from timestep_lv natural right join (SELECT SBSNUMBER, DISPERSALMEASUREMENTID, TIMESTEPINMINUTES as timestepminutes, N, REPLICATES, MEAN, MEDIAN, MINIMUM, MAXIMUM, STDDEVIATION, STDERROR, P_COMMENT, CREATED_WHEN, UPDATED_WHEN, BATCHID, UPDATEDWHO, REFERENCEID, METHODID, TAXONID, ORIGREFERENCEID, HABITATTYPEID, GEOREFID, VALID, VALIDSINCE, VALIDUNTIL, LEDAID, DISPERSALID, DISPERSALPOTENTIAL, ORIGINALDISPERSALVECTORVALUE, DISPERSALVECTORID, ORIGINALDISPERSALTYPEVALUE, DISPERSALTYPEID, DISPERSALUNITID FROM buoyancy_dispersal natural join taxontosbsassignment)
 WHERE valid IN (-2, 1, 2, -8, 2, -8))) byc ON sbs_dis.sbs_sbsnumber = byc.byc_sbsnumber)) GROUP BY sbs_sbsnumber, sbs_sbsname, dtlv_name, dvlv_name, dvglv_genname, dglv_genname) ORDER BY sbs_sbsname
